## <a href="http://36kr.com/p/5245772.html?ktm_source=feed" target="_blank">最前线丨盒马全线接入饿了么平台，持续降低物流成本</a>
2019-09-12 10:32:14   <a href="#" id="a_1c69c22cd50711e9b14000163c8b9390" onclick="onClickAction('2019-09','1c69c22cd50711e9b14000163c8b9390')">[收起]</a>
<div class="collector_content" id="div_1c69c22cd50711e9b14000163c8b9390" onclick="onClickAction('2019-09','1c69c22cd50711e9b14000163c8b9390')">
<p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">9月12日，</span><strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">36氪获悉，</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">盒马鲜生将于当月</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">全量上线饿了么平台，共涉及全国21座城市超过150家门店。</span></strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">今后，盒马用户通过饿了么平台也能下单，享受</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">30分钟送上门服务。</span><br/></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">36氪了解到，<strong>盒马接入饿了么平台前期，配送服务依旧由盒马自己来提供；随着合作深入，双方在零售品类、配送和消费</strong><strong>者个性化服务等方面将有进一步协同。</strong></span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;"></span></p><p>提高配送人效、降低配送成本是盒马当下的重心之一。生鲜领域本身对物流要求较高，还面临着高昂的仓储成本，在这两项重压下，盈利成为亟待解决的问题。观研天下报告数据显示，典型的社区生鲜店毛利率为19.6%，损耗率达8%，低毛利率、高损耗率与门店高人工与租金费用，是社区生鲜经营的主要矛盾。</p><p>盒马的优势在于，门店即前置仓，从门店发货能提高物流效率；线上订单量占比60%能提高商品周转率、降低损耗。全量接入饿了么平台后，盒马将获得更多线上流量，带来线上订单量的增长。<span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">但在物流成本方面，盒马仍有改进的空间。</span></p><p>此前盒马已有意调整物流环节以降低物流成本，比如提高配送人效、对包装材料二次利用。<span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">随着</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">盒马与饿了么合作深入，<strong>饿了么如果参与到配送环节中，盒马将有可能持续降低配送环节的人工成本，而饿了么也将收获更多配送订单。</strong></span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">艾媒咨询于今年5月发布的《2019中国即时配送市场研究报告》显示，蜂鸟配送新零售订单在2018年下半年同比增长185%，医药健康订单增幅超过500%。</span></p><p>（本文题图来自饿了么）</p><p><br/></p>
</div>
<script src="../../collectorjs.js"></script>
<script>
window.onload=function(){
    let storage = window.localStorage;
    var local = JSON.parse(storage.getItem('month_2019-09'));
    if (local) {
        var div_list = document.getElementsByClassName("collector_content");
        for (i = 0; i < div_list.length; i++) {
            var item = div_list[i];
            var id = item.id.replace('div_', '');
            if(local.indexOf(id) > -1){
                var eObject = document.getElementById('div_'+id);
                var aObject = document.getElementById('a_'+id);
                eObject.style.display = 'none';
                aObject.innerHTML = '[展开]';
            }
        }
    }
}
</script>

<div class="collector_content" id="div_c4af7f9bd50c11e9b14000163c8b9390" onclick="onClickAction('2019-09','c4af7f9bd50c11e9b14000163c8b9390')">
<p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, <script>
window.onload=function(){
    let storage = window.localStorage;
    var local = JSON.parse(storage.getItem('month_2019-09'));
    if (local) {
        var div_list = document.getElementsByClassName("collector_content");
        for (i = 0; i < div_list.length; i++) {
            var item = div_list[i];
            var id = item.id.replace('div_', '');

                var eObject = document.getElementById('div_'+id);
                var aObject = document.getElementById('a_'+id);
                eObject.style.display = 'none';
                aObject.innerHTML = '[展开]';
            }
        }
    }
}
</script>
## <a href="http://36kr.com/p/5245772.html?ktm_source=feed" target="_blank">最前线丨盒马全量接入饿了么平台，全国21城超150家门店当月上线</a>
2019-09-12 10:32:14   <a href="#" id="a_0c5c715fd50d11e9b14000163c8b9390" onclick="onClickAction('2019-09','0c5c715fd50d11e9b14000163c8b9390')">[收起]</a>
<div class="collector_content" id="div_0c5c715fd50d11e9b14000163c8b9390" onclick="onClickAction('2019-09','0c5c715fd50d11e9b14000163c8b9390')">
<p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">9月12日，</span><strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">36氪获悉，</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">盒马鲜生将于当月</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">全量上线饿了么平台，共涉及全国21座城市超过150家门店。</span></strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">今后，盒马用户通过饿了么平台也能下单，享受</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">30分钟送上门服务。</span><br/></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">36氪了解到，<strong>盒马接入饿了么平台前期，配送服务依旧由盒马自己来提供；随着合作深入，双方在零售品类、配送和消费</strong><strong>者个性化服务等方面将有进一步协同。</strong></span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;"></span></p><p>生鲜领域本身对物流要求较高，还面临着高昂的仓储成本，在这两项重压下，盈利成为亟待解决的问题。观研天下报告数据显示，典型的社区生鲜店毛利率为19.6%，损耗率达8%，低毛利率、高损耗率与门店高人工与租金费用，是社区生鲜经营的主要矛盾。</p><p>盒马的优势在于，门店即前置仓，从门店发货能提高物流效率；线上订单量占比60%能提高商品周转率、降低损耗。全量接入饿了么平台后，盒马将获得更多线上流量，带来线上订单量的增长。</p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">随着</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">盒马与饿了么合作深入，饿了么如果参与到配送环节中，将收获更多配送订单。</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">艾媒咨询于今年5月发布的《2019中国即时配送市场研究报告》显示，蜂鸟配送新零售订单在2018年下半年同比增长185%，医药健康订单增幅超过500%。</span></p><p>（本文题图来自饿了么）</p><p><br/></p>
</div>

## <a href="http://36kr.com/p/5245425.html?ktm_source=feed" target="_blank">不止于「真人吃鸡」，「巨硬互动」要用物联网互动娱乐平台打造「新」线下真人情景游戏</a>
2019-09-12 10:31:03   <a href="#" id="a_8271c68ed50511e9b14000163c8b9390" onclick="onClickAction('2019-09','8271c68ed50511e9b14000163c8b9390')">[收起]</a>
<div class="collector_content" id="div_8271c68ed50511e9b14000163c8b9390" onclick="onClickAction('2019-09','8271c68ed50511e9b14000163c8b9390')">
<p>根据中国演出行业协会发布《中国演出市场年度报告》，我国线下演出市场规模近些年一直处于小幅升降，没有超过500亿，对比欧美日韩市场，国内的线下演出的潜力是被严重低估的。<strong>不仅如此，线上娱乐产品巨头垄断的市场以及持续收紧的过审政策也使得企业纷纷思考线下娱乐的可能，市场规模未来有望突破式增长。</strong></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">看准线下娱乐市场发展前景，「<a href="http://www.xdlsc168.com/" target="_blank">巨硬互动</a>」联合创始人兼CEO</span>何赛<span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">同其他创始人一拍即合，<strong>成立以物联网为基础，提供虚实结合的线下互动娱乐产品及平台的「巨硬互动」</strong>，并且在2018年选择打造基于网红游戏「绝地求生」的线下实景娱乐产品<strong>，以「真人吃鸡」的场景切入线下沉浸娱乐市场。同年，「巨硬互动」中标芒果TV《勇敢的世界》项目，成为其独家系统合作商</strong>。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">关于为何选择绝地求生真人吃鸡作为线下情景娱乐的突破口，「巨硬互动」告诉36氪，在项目准备之前，2016至2017年，「绝地」及守望等 FPS 类 PVP 游戏都非常火爆，而两者相比，<strong>绝地的游戏内容包括地图设定、对战模式、以及道具系统更利于线下转化与铺设。</strong></span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">相比于「真人CS」只提供对战的单一玩法，线下真人吃鸡带来了<strong>舔包、捡道具、虚拟小地图等多种新创意，升级了玩家的游戏体验</strong>。但何赛同时也表示，「巨硬互动」所想提供给线下沉浸娱乐的<strong>并不只是体感level up版的真人吃鸡或真人CS，而是基于IOT的互动娱乐硬件设备及软件平台，「新」线下枪战游戏只算作是「巨硬互动」平台落地的第一个场景以及革新线下竞技娱乐的第一步</strong>。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">「巨硬互动」打算利用物联网互动娱乐平台为线下沉浸娱乐带来<strong>两大「新」变化</strong>：</span></p><address><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">「新体验」，“虚拟+现实”结合，让线下沉浸娱乐比线上更加刺激。</span></p></address><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">还是以「绝地求生」为例，由于设备的限制，真人情景对抗很难真实还原游戏小地图、道具掉落玩法，而一旦剥离了这些，所谓的线下吃鸡就很容易变成已经烂大街的真人CS，如何在真人对抗的「刺激战场」上<strong>保留虚拟端的多种玩法</strong>成为了许多线下游戏的难题。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">针对这一痛点，「巨硬互动」将互动娱乐平台设计为四部分：<strong>智能可穿戴设备、交互道具、C端App、总控平台。</strong></span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;"></span></p><p><img src="https://pic.36krcnd.com/201909/11082902/3tpi4ctxr5wpea6u.jpg!heading" data-img-size-val="718,621" width="718"/></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;"></span><br/></p><p><img src="https://pic.36krcnd.com/201909/11082959/g258xmj15o2ghn00.jpg!heading" data-img-size-val="800,525"/></p><p label="图片描述" classname="img-desc" class="img-desc" style="">智能可穿戴设备及便携式激光发射器</p><p><strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">利用物联技术，</span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">将用户身上的智能可穿戴设备（例如头盔，防弹衣或其他配件）和配有「巨硬互动」独立研发的可拆卸激光发射器的外挂互动道具串联，再加上用户手头的C端app显示地图或敌人标识，“虚拟”+“现实”联动，「绝地求生」线上玩法复刻的部分难点被击破</span></strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;"></span></p><p><img src="https://pic.36krcnd.com/201909/11083105/mjlx8bv5v6wvw08n.jpg!heading" data-img-size-val="641,309"/></p><p class="img-desc">巨硬互动线下吃鸡app虚拟地图界面</p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">不仅如此，「巨硬互动」后端SaaS总控平台能够对玩家血量、道具功能及游戏规则进行监管与调整，并且可以直接在穿戴设备端或者C端APP直接对玩家进行指导和提示，“傻瓜式”操作大大减少了传统线下娱乐布局所需要的人力成本。</span><br/></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">同理，不局限于吃鸡场景，运营商还可以借助「巨硬互动」所提供的硬件及系统，<strong>前端自定义穿戴设备、交互道具的物化模型，中端DIY设计玩家APP端的内容显示，后端制定合理的游戏规则，生成属于自己的爆款线下游戏。</strong></span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">虽然游戏内容可以实现客制化，单CEO何赛也表示，基于现在的设备，具体能落地什么游戏内容还是有所限制，<strong>大多以FPS类型为主</strong>，不过「巨硬互动」将会在之后对产品进行迭代，以便更多更好的线上游戏内容能够进行线下复刻。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;"></span></p><p><img src="https://pic.36krcnd.com/201909/11083403/rbxb3jg9xlcetwn1.jpg!heading" data-img-size-val="1440,1080"/></p><p class="img-desc">装备及道具一览</p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">现阶段的「吃鸡」场景，「巨硬互动」对其系统及道具<strong>维持着三个月一大更，一个月一小更的迭代频率</strong>，为防止一些玩家落地成盒影响用户体验而最近添加了「王者吃鸡」新游戏</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">玩</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">法</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">，玩家在「王者吃鸡」模式内，可以像在<strong>传统MOBA游戏内一样，不限次数复活及升级装备</strong>。</span></p><address><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">「新地点」，突破场地限制天花板，盘活商用低效及公园闲置空间。</span></p></address><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">「巨硬互动」选择与城市商超或公园合作，<strong>借用其闲置及低效空间打造属于自己的线下游戏场地</strong>。对于场地合作方来说，<strong>不仅场地闲置率得到改善，线下真人情景游戏的入住无疑还能为其创造一定的客流量</strong>；而对于「巨硬互动」来说，商超、公园的合作能够<strong>减少其场地布置成本</strong>，而且多形态的游戏空间意味着<strong>多种类的地图</strong>，能够有效打破以往真人竞技游戏的场地天花板。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">「巨硬互动」线下产品的主要客户流来自B端企业团队（团建活动）以及C端加盟店会员、复购粉丝、大众点评推荐来的散客，<strong>客单价在人均200元左右</strong>。截止目前，<strong>「巨硬科技」已经拥有了20家加盟店，并且打算在年底扩展到50家</strong>。按店铺铺大小的不同，每场比赛可容纳的人数也不同，一般一场比赛持续一个半小时，周末每日店均能接待5-6批（30-50人）玩家，<strong>多数店铺能在三个月内回本</strong>。据CEO介绍，「巨硬互动」现有系统<strong>能容纳200人同时同局作战</strong>。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;"></span></p><p><img src="https://pic.36krcnd.com/201909/11082404/nn21d54vgbnnye1l.jpg!heading" data-img-size-val="4608,3456"/></p><p class="img-desc">芒果粉丝节「巨硬互动」真人吃鸡玩家照</p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">据了解，<strong>「巨硬互动」正在与苏州丽丰购物中心达成合作关系，新门店将于11月落地，与苏州环球港、北京798园区、长沙浔龙河特色小镇的邀请入驻也在洽谈中</strong>。核心团队曾与万达广场、吾悦广场、银泰等知名地产品牌合作多个线下娱乐场地，其合作模式多为<strong>以项目流量带入抵扣租金成本的模式</strong>。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">在项目前景方面，何赛告诉36氪，「巨硬互动」的产品还处于“<strong>人无我有</strong>”的状态，与传统真人CS相比，</span><strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">客单价达到了</span>200%<span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">的提升</span></strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">，并且将在未来几年都有较高的增长空间。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">线下的沉浸娱乐产品研发常会遇到内<strong>容缺乏、参照系难找、迭代难做的情况</strong>。「巨硬互动」选择已有名气且玩法多样的线上游戏IP做线下移植，<strong>既为自己的产品更新找到标的，又能获得IP自带的一定用户流量</strong>。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">同许多线下娱乐产品一样，「巨硬互动」现阶段需要注重的问题是基于如何提高线下吃鸡产品的复购率及会员转化率。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">复购率在于两点，<strong>场地的复购和产品的复购</strong>。就场地而言，「巨硬互动」的线下吃鸡游戏单次参与在人均200元左右，算是偏贵，且玩家在体验过游戏内容后，<strong>往往就对同一场景丧失了新鲜感</strong>。</span></p><p>就产品而言，虽然有进行产品迭代，但由于现行设备的限制，<strong>线下吃鸡依然无法完全复刻线上如跳伞、飙车的玩法</strong>。<strong>而且现阶段平台只有「真人吃鸡」游戏，并没有更多其他的游戏类型可供选择</strong>，这也很难吸引更多用户入场。</p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">「巨硬互动」也发现了场景新鲜度的痛点，所以其现阶段计划的重心就是<strong>拓展更多类型场景地图（尤其是To B端）及游戏模式</strong>，同时打造加盟商及用户会员运营系统，组建城市场地联盟，让<strong>一个城市里用户可以自主选择联盟内的各个「地图」和「游戏模式」</strong>。此外还在规划与某全息互动厂商合作共同打造沉浸式吃鸡主题</span>乐园<span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">，将全息投影、裸眼3D、AR等技术引入巨硬物联网平台系统。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">团队建设方面，CEO何赛，UCLA经济及数学学士，中国人民大学MBA，具有投资银行背景，<strong>长期关注线下沉浸式娱乐项目</strong>。联合创始人张铭，雪豹突击队退伍军官，具有10年线下娱乐项目运营经验，曾创建C+品牌。团队核心成员多有线下娱乐、物联网技术研发及互联网产品开发运营等相关</span>经验<span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">此前，巨硬互动在2018年7月，获土流网CEO伍勇的200万元seed轮投资。现在，巨硬互动正寻求下一轮融资，主要用于完善全国加盟商及用户会员运营系统和渠道推广，形成沉浸式玩法+物联网智能设备+移动互联网的体系。</span></p>
</div>

## <a href="http://36kr.com/p/5245680.html?ktm_source=feed" target="_blank">退出“烧钱”的新零售，超市赚钱的思路该变了</a>
2019-09-12 10:02:05   <a href="#" id="a_74d573b8d50111e9b14000163c8b9390" onclick="onClickAction('2019-09','74d573b8d50111e9b14000163c8b9390')">[收起]</a>
<div class="collector_content" id="div_74d573b8d50111e9b14000163c8b9390" onclick="onClickAction('2019-09','74d573b8d50111e9b14000163c8b9390')">
<p>编者按：本文来自微信公众号“<a href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/4QGLxkIpDsRmu6J-Eu9A3g" target="_blank">赢商网</a>”（ID：winshang），作者陈绮琪，36氪经授权发布。</p><section data-label="powered by xmt.cn" data-tools="新媒体管家"></section><section data-role="outer" label="Powered by 135editor.com"><section data-id="89968" data-tools="135编辑器"><section data-color="#0080FF" data-custom="#0080FF" data-id="86449"><section><section><section><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">今年以来，很多超市企业重新聚焦超市主业，逐步退出“烧钱”业务，业绩回暖了吗？</span></p></section></section><section><section><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">近两年，不少超市都效仿盒马鲜生推出“超市+餐饮”业态，希望能找到新的业绩增长点，然而其转型效果并不理想，绝大部分企业的业绩依旧没有起色，甚至“不增反跌”。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">进入2019年，超市的业绩有没有回暖呢？</span></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section>据赢商网统计，高鑫零售、永辉、步步高、家家悦、人人乐、卜蜂莲花等  <strong>13家超市上市企业</strong>  <strong>2019年1-6月</strong>  共实现  <strong>营业收入1645.1亿元</strong>  ，同比上涨5.69%，涨幅同比增长了1个百分点；合计  <strong>总净利润为40.03亿元</strong>  ，同比下降1.16%，与去年同期13.57%的涨幅相比，大幅下滑。其中，8家企业实现营收、净利双增长，2家营收、净利均下跌，2家增收不增利，1家营收下降但净利增长。</section><section><br/>  </section><section><img src="https://img.36krcdn.com/20190911/v2_1568209794125_img_000"/>  </section><section><img src="https://img.36krcdn.com/20190911/v2_1568209794169_img_000"/>  </section><section><img src="https://img.36krcdn.com/20190911/v2_1568209794213_img_000"/>  </section><section><section><section><h2 label="一级标题">01&nbsp;<strong style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">营收PK：</strong><strong style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">步步高半年营收首破百亿，</strong><strong style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">人人乐和华联综超连跌三年</strong></h2></section></section></section><h3 label="二级标题" style=""><strong><strong><strong>步步高半年营收首破百亿 永辉“紧追”高鑫零售</strong></strong></strong></h3><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">今年上半年，超市行业格局十分稳定，企业营收排名与去年一致，  </span><strong style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">高鑫零售和永辉超市依然稳居营收第一、第二位</strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">  ，分别是543.96亿元、411.76亿元，与其他企业拉开较大距离；联华超市和步步高以134.88亿元、100.7亿元分别位列第三、第四，上述企业也是上半年营收超过百亿的四家企业，其中  </span><strong style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">步步高是首次跨进半年营收百亿军团</strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">  。</span></p><section>值得注意的是，高鑫零售近几年的营收增长明显放缓，而永辉超市则以约20%的涨幅稳步上涨，两者在营收方面的差距已由2016年的512亿元缩减到2018年的308亿元。</section><h3 label="二级标题" style=""><strong><strong><strong>10家超市营收增长 人人乐和华联综超连跌三年</strong></strong></strong></h3><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">上半年，实现营收增长的超市有10家，较去年同期多了1家。其中，  </span><strong style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">营收增幅最大</strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">  </span><strong style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">的依然是永辉超市</strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">  ，达到19.71%，主要得益于新开门店数持续增加，同时老店客单价增加，销售额实现稳步上升。此外，家家悦的营收涨幅也达到16.68%，主要系其同店收入增长、新店发展及非同一控制下合并河北家家悦所致。</span></p><p>联华超市和北京京客隆的营收变动则由去年同期的负增长变为今年的正增长，联华超市将其归功于集团新增网点及对既存网点的转型改造取得成效。</p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">不难发现，新店拓展以及同店销售增长是影响营收增长的主要因素。</span></p><section>值得注意的是，  <strong>人人乐和华联综超的半年营收已经连续三年下滑</strong>  ，其中华联综超将营收下跌归因于门店客流量下降，人人乐对此不做解释。</section><section><section><section><h2 label="一级标题">02&nbsp;<strong style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">净利PK：</strong><strong style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">永辉净利恢复增长，</strong><strong style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">新华都因关店亏逾1亿</strong></h2></section></section></section><h3 label="二级标题" style=""><strong><strong><strong>11家超市实现盈利 新华都因大规模关店亏掉1个亿</strong></strong></strong></h3><section></section><p>今年1-6月，共有11家超市实现盈利，其中  <strong>高鑫零售以17.66亿元稳居净利润榜首</strong>  ，永辉超市以净利13.69亿元位居第二，这也是上半年净利润突破10亿元的两家企业。  步步高、家家悦和红旗连锁的净利润均超过2亿元，三江购物则超过1亿元 ，中百集团、卜蜂莲花、联华超市、华联综超和京客隆均不超1亿元。</p><p>与此同时，也有两家企业录得  <strong>亏损</strong>  ，分别是  <strong>人人乐和新华都</strong>  。据了解，人人乐亏损是因为上半年销售及毛利下降，以及新店亏损。新华都则是因为优化门店结构而关闭了48家门店，产生赔偿损失、装修长摊余额一次性摊销损失等金额约1.61亿元，影响了业绩。</p><section>据了解，人人乐因连续两年亏损再次“披星戴帽”，股票简称变更为“*ST人乐”，若今年继续亏损，其将面临终止上市的风险。  此外，今年7月中旬，人人乐“易主”，控股股东“浩明公司”拟将其持有的上市公司8800万股股票（占上市公司股本总额的20.00%）转让给曲江文化。</section><section><img src="https://img.36krcdn.com/20190911/v2_1568209794322_img_000"/>  </section><p label="图片描述" classname="img-desc" class="img-desc">图片来源：赢商网</p><section>处于“水深火热”之中的还有  卜蜂莲花，  要约方C.P. Holding （BVI）Investment Company Limited已经要求董事会提出建议将公司私有化，有业内人士猜测，这或与卜蜂莲花盈利不佳有关。</section><h3 label="二级标题" style=""><strong style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;"><strong><strong>9家超市净利增长 永辉甩掉“云创”后业绩重回轨道</strong></strong></strong><br/></h3><p>今年上半年，共有9家超市的净利润实现增长，不过与去年同期相比，超市整体的净利涨幅有所回落。</p><section>上半年净利润增长最为明显的是  <strong>三江购物</strong>  ，  <strong>涨幅为97.04%</strong>  ，而去年同期净利润是同比下降13.81%。据悉，三江购物上半年净利润大涨主要得益于转让全资孙公司杭州浙海华地获得收益。此外，“甩掉”云创包袱的  <strong>永辉超市</strong>  业绩也恢复增长，  <strong>上半年净利润同比大涨46.69%</strong>  。</section><section><img src="https://img.36krcdn.com/20190911/v2_1568209794364_img_000"/>  </section><p label="图片描述" classname="img-desc" class="img-desc">图片来源：三江购物</p><p>值得注意的是，上半年有4家超市的净利润下滑，除了上述两家录得亏损的人人乐和新华都，还有中百集团和卜蜂莲花。据  悉，中百集团去年净利得以大涨237.05%，主要是因为2017年同期实施完成江夏中百购物广场资产证券  化项目以及2018年中百仓储因珞狮路卖场拆迁补偿。</p><section><strong>卜蜂莲花</strong>  上半年净利下滑主要是受采用香港财务报告准则16号的影响，共计  <strong>减少利润约7940万元</strong>  ，以及因为新店扩张带来的销售及商品利润尚未完全覆盖新增店铺的运营成本。2017年，卜蜂莲花通过裁员降低成本实现扭亏，但2018年再次陷入亏损，今年上半年，卜蜂莲花加大裁员力度，半年减员700+人，但上半年净利润依然同比大跌七成，故裁员扭亏的措施是否还能奏效尚有待考察。</section><section><section><section><h2 label="一级标题">03&nbsp;<strong style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">行业发展趋势：</strong><strong style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">脱坑+整合+全渠道+中小业态</strong></h2></section></section></section><h3 label="二级标题" style=""><strong><strong><strong>逐步退出“烧钱”赛道</strong></strong></strong></h3><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">2017年，不少超市推出“超市+餐饮”业态谋求转型，然而这一举措并没有推动各企业的业绩增长，反而成了前进的绊脚石。</span></p><p>去年，新华都、永辉超市开始“脱坑”——新华都出售福建新盒（即福建盒马鲜生）40.50%股权予杭州阿里巴巴泽泰，永辉超市将连年亏损的云创业务剥离出上市公司体系。进入2019年，  <strong>退出“超市+餐饮”业务的超市也越来越多</strong>  ：</p><p><strong>●</strong> 4月12日晚，  <strong>三江购物</strong>  宣布拟以3000万元  <strong>转让全资子公司杭州浙海华地</strong>  （主要运营杭州盒马门店）100%股权予杭州盒马，杭州浙海华地2018年1-12月净亏损1073.25万元。</p><section><strong>●</strong> 5月31日，  <strong>高鑫零售</strong>  宣布，大润发中国以500万美元向上海润盒  <strong>出售海南盒马</strong>  全部股权。2018年5月28日至2018年12月31日，海南盒马净亏损972万元。</section><section><img src="https://img.36krcdn.com/20190911/v2_1568209794400_img_000"/>  </section><p label="图片描述" classname="img-desc" class="img-desc">图片来源：盒马官方微博</p><p><strong>●</strong> 6月27日，  <strong>新华都</strong>  宣布以1元  <strong>转让海物会51%股权</strong>  予新界餐饮，海物会2018年亏损1582.63万元，2019年1-5月亏损405.39万元。</p><p>不难发现，大部分“超市+餐饮”业态目前仍是处于亏损状态，对企业业绩增长并无贡献，若把些包袱“甩掉”，企业业绩压力也能得以减轻。</p><h3 label="二级标题" style=""><strong><strong><strong>重新聚焦超市主业、加速布局中小业态</strong></strong></strong></h3><section></section><p>不同于前两年“疯狂追捧”无人零售和“超市+餐饮”业态，今年上半年零售市场及时止损理智回归，不少超市默默做回老本行，  <strong>聚焦超市主业</strong>  。永辉超市取得了对百佳永辉的实际控制权，百佳永辉门店正式并入永辉超市系统，但百佳永辉目前还处于亏损阶段，上半年净利润亏损1481.82万元。高鑫零售旗下大润发、欧尚双品牌整合初步完成，门店IT系统升级整合也于4月中完成。</p><section>与此同时，多家超市继续  <strong>推出新品牌</strong>  ，进一步完善自身业态布局，如新华都与淘鲜达合作推出  <strong>“邻聚菜场”</strong>  ，步步高再推社区生鲜品牌  <strong>“汇米生鲜”</strong>  ，永辉推出定位社区生鲜的  <strong>永辉mini</strong>  ，卜蜂莲花推出精品生活超市  <strong>BAZZAR</strong>  和  <strong>优鲜超市</strong>  ......据观察，上述新业态开出的均为小面积门店，约为几百到两三千平方米，且大都主打生鲜零售，明显瞄准了人们的日常生活所需。</section><h3 label="二级标题" style=""><strong><strong><strong>持续发力全渠道数字化运营</strong></strong></strong></h3><p>近年来，电商渠道的发展对实体零售产生了不小的冲击，线上线下的边界也变得越来越模糊，为了抗衡电商冲击，发展全渠道零售、推进数字化改造成为超市企业的共同选择：</p><p><strong>●</strong> <strong>高鑫零售B2C业务</strong>  已经步入正轨，旗下所有大润发和欧尚门店均接入淘鲜达，配送半径从3公里扩大到5公里。大润发e路发APP期内实现持续增长，预计今年增长50%。</p><section></section><p><strong>●</strong> <strong>永辉超市</strong>  完成  <strong>社区团购</strong>  、永辉超市  <strong>小程序</strong>  的开发落地与推广，其中社区团购已在300 多家门店推广应用。</p><p><strong>●</strong> <strong>家家悦</strong>  开始启动  <strong>SAP 系统项目</strong>  ，以提升企业的数字化能力；通过成立团队及与第三方合作，启动了线上线下一体化融合项目，提供到家服务和到店服务。</p><section></section><p><strong>●</strong> <strong>三江购物</strong>  全面升级  <strong>阿里云 POS</strong>  ，门店全面推行自助 POS 机、新增自助打秤的场景，减少消费者排队时间。</p><section></section><section><strong>●</strong> <strong>中百集团</strong>  大力推进  <strong>O2O到家业务</strong>  ，仓储公司多渠道推进多点会员拉新，多措并举提升会员积极性、增加复购；超市公司“饿了么”新增上线119家，“美团”新增上线80家。</section><section></section><section></section><h3 label="二级标题" style=""><strong><strong><strong>行业整合进一步加快</strong></strong></strong></h3><p>进入2019年，超市行业整合加快，  <strong>收购、入股的消息不断传出</strong>  ：</p><p><strong>●</strong> 1月底，步步高收购家润多22家门店，后者门店主要分布在长沙、益阳、常德、衡阳、郴州等地。</p><p><strong>●</strong> 3月份，物美、家家悦先后接管华润万家北京5家大卖场门店（原来Tesco）、山东7家门店。</p><p><strong>●</strong> 3月底，永辉宣布计划要约收购中百集团10.14%股份，拟将持股比例从目前29.86%提高至最多不超过40%，有望上位第一大股东，目前该交易方案已经通过反垄断审查。</p><section><strong>●</strong> 6月25日，物美、步步高分别以70.75亿元和15.72亿元现金入股重庆商社集团，该交易已获得国家市场监督管理总局同意。</section><section><img src="https://img.36krcdn.com/20190911/v2_1568209794520_img_000"/>  </section><p label="图片描述" classname="img-desc" class="img-desc">图片来源：步步高时间</p><section>据观察，步步高、物美和家家悦通过收购巩固了各自在大本营市场的地位，而永辉要约收购中百集团主要是为了拓展华中市场，物美、步步高入股重庆商社则是借曲线实现对西南零售市场的扩张。</section><h2 label="一级标题"><strong>-结语-</strong></h2><h2 label="一级标题"></h2><section></section><section></section><section>纵观超市上半年业绩数据可以发现，企业规模断层依然存在，高鑫零售和永辉超市在营收、净利上继续遥遥领先，但两者之间的差距正在逐步缩小。  另一方面，超市企业开始回归理性，重新聚焦超市主业，同时逐步退出“烧钱”业务，今年整体业绩有望较去年有明显改善。</section><section><section><section></section></section></section>
</div>

## <a href="https://www.blog.google/inside-google/company-announcements/recover-together/" target="_blank">The courage to change: sharing resources for recovery</a>
2019-09-12 10:00:00   <a href="#" id="a_c3fa2633d54511e9b14000163c8b9390" onclick="onClickAction('2019-09','c3fa2633d54511e9b14000163c8b9390')">[收起]</a>
<div class="collector_content" id="div_c3fa2633d54511e9b14000163c8b9390" onclick="onClickAction('2019-09','c3fa2633d54511e9b14000163c8b9390')">
<html><head></head><body><div class="block-paragraph"><div class="rich-text"><p>I didn't know what recovery meant until a friend asked me if I was still "in recovery." Confused, I responded, “Yes, I’m still not drinking, if that's what you mean.” I know now what I didn’t know then: Recovery means life after substance abuse. It means having a clear mind and a healthy body. It means having the foresight to say no to alcohol. It means having the mental clarity to thrive at work and the desire to live a fuller, happier, complete life. </p><p>As someone who has struggled with addiction and embarked on a journey toward recovery, I am so proud that Google is marking <a href="https://recoverymonth.gov/">National Recovery Month</a> with a new site, <a href="http://g.co/recovertogether">Recover Together</a>. I participate in a recovery group at Google and know how important it is for this community to be connected. As part of Google’s <a href="https://www.blog.google/outreach-initiatives/public-policy/national-drug-take-back-day/">ongoing efforts</a> to combat the opioid crisis, today we’re taking an additional step to support those in recovery.</p><p>Too many of us have experienced firsthand the devastating impact of addiction—with our friends, colleagues, family members and loved ones. From the first time I filled my water bottle with alcohol and brought it to school at only 14 years old, to the many times I blacked out and woke up in the back seat of my car in surprising locations, I know how deeply addiction affected my life and worried my family.</p><p>More than 21 million Americans struggle with substance use. But it is treatable: An estimated 1 out of 14 American adults is in recovery. In fact, people come to Google every day to seek information on addiction treatment, prevention and recovery. Just last month, we saw an all-time high in search interest for “rehab near me,” “addiction treatment near me” and “how to help an addict.”</p></div></div><div class="block-image_full_width"><div class="article-module h-c-page"><div class="h-c-grid"><figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 "><img alt="Top searched questions on addiction" src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/images/Top_Questions_on_Addiction.max-1000x1000.png"/></figure></div></div></div><div class="block-paragraph"><div class="rich-text"><p>Starting today, you can come to Google to find recovery resources all in one place, beginning with a video series from those in recovery. I felt less alone when hearing others share their stories, and I am grateful to be able to do the same here.</p></div></div><div class="block-video"><div class="h-c-page h-c-page--mobile-full-bleed"><div class="h-c-grid"><div class="h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col-l--12 "><div class="article-module article-video "><figure><a class="h-c-video h-c-video--marquee" data-glue-modal-disabled-on-mobile="true" data-glue-modal-trigger="uni-modal-I0tPEmlhLZg-" href="https://youtube.com/watch?v=I0tPEmlhLZg"><div class="article-video__aspect-image" style="background-image: url(https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/images/Shawna_V8.00_02_12_07.Still001.max-1000x1000.jpg);"><span class="h-u-visually-hidden">Shawna tells her story in a YouTube video.</span></div><svg class="h-c-video__play h-c-icon h-c-icon--color-white" role="img"><use xlink:href="#mi-youtube-icon"></use></svg></a></figure></div></div></div></div><div class="h-c-modal--video" data-glue-modal="uni-modal-I0tPEmlhLZg-" data-glue-modal-close-label="Close Dialog"><a class="glue-yt-video" data-glue-yt-video-autoplay="true" data-glue-yt-video-height="99%" data-glue-yt-video-vid="I0tPEmlhLZg" data-glue-yt-video-width="100%" href="https://youtube.com/watch?v=I0tPEmlhLZg" ng-cloak=""></a></div></div><div class="block-paragraph_with_image"><div class="article-module h-c-page"><div class="h-c-grid uni-paragraph-wrap"><div class="uni-paragraph h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--8 h-c-grid__col-m--6 h-c-grid__col-l--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-2 h-c-grid__col-m--offset-3 h-c-grid__col-l--offset-3"><figure class="article-image--wrap-small "><img alt="Recovery locator tool" src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-uniblog-publish-prod/images/StLouis_MO.max-1000x1000.png"/><figcaption class="article-image__caption "><div class="rich-text"><p>Our new Recovery Locator Tool in Maps. </p></div></figcaption></figure><div class="rich-text"><p>We’re also launching two new Google Maps locator tools that will connect people with crucial recovery resources, including: </p><ul><li><p><b><a href="https://recovertogether.withgoogle.com/#resource-map">Recovery Locator Tool</a>: </b>A map with locations of more than 83,000 recovery support meetings such as AA, NA, Al-Anon and SmartRecovery, and other services such as school-based and family support. These take place at more than 33,000 community centers, churches, and other spaces—put in your address and you’ll see many recovery services are in your area or wherever you’re traveling.</p></li><li><p><b><a href="https://recovertogether.withgoogle.com/treatment/#naloxone">Naloxone Locator Tool</a>: </b>A special locator tool will show you locations where you can get Naloxone, the life-saving opioid overdose-reversal drug, without a prescription. All you have to do is type “Naloxone near me” or “Narcan near me” into the search bar in the tool. It already includes 20,000 pharmacies (including CVS, Rite-Aid and Walgreens) in 50 states, and we’ll continue to add local clinics and independent pharmacies. The site will also have more information about the availability and life-saving capability of this medication. Soon, these locations will also be searchable directly in Google Maps.</p></li></ul></div></div></div></div></div><div class="block-paragraph"><div class="rich-text"><p>Finding recovery is a personal journey, and I am so grateful to work for a company that is making resources available to those who need them. In addition to these new tools, the site points to many other resources for those seeking treatment, including <a href="https://www.drugabuse.gov/taps/#/">a self-assessment screener</a> from the National Institute of Drug Abuse and state-specific Helpline resources and hotlines. </p><p>To anyone at the beginning stages of recovery: This process is hard and tiring and challenging and you do not need to figure this all out alone. From the moment I first connected to the Employee Assistance Program counselor at Google who helped me confront the reality of my addiction, my life has changed in ways that at one time seemed unimaginable. I teach yoga. I run marathons. My life has been enriched by others in the recovery community. My sorrow has been replaced with a joy I never thought possible. And today, my hope is that anyone seeking recovery can find the same help and resources through Google I wanted so many years ago. Recovery is difficult, and it is so much better when we’re all in it together.<br/></p></div></div></body></html>
</div>

## <a href="https://www.oschina.net/news/109807/plua-0-1-released" target="_blank">pLua 0.1发布，Lua 性能分析工具</a>
2019-09-12 09:12:25   <a href="#" id="a_b04ac789d50311e9b14000163c8b9390" onclick="onClickAction('2019-09','b04ac789d50311e9b14000163c8b9390')">[收起]</a>
<div class="collector_content" id="div_b04ac789d50311e9b14000163c8b9390" onclick="onClickAction('2019-09','b04ac789d50311e9b14000163c8b9390')">
pLua Lua 性能分析工具 原理 类似于 gperftools，通过定时器信号回调查看调用栈，来定位调用的热点 特性 简单，只需几行代码，即可输出结果 准确，相比 lua hook，定时采样的方式更能准确捕获 lua 执行的热点 轻量，因为是采样的，相比直接按行 lua hook，能最小程度影响宿主程序的运行 直观，输出调用图，能直观的看到热...
</div>

## <a href="http://36kr.com/p/5244981.html?ktm_source=feed" target="_blank">更名「大麦」，“头部玩家”「科发源」意在全球植发市场</a>
2019-09-12 09:09:09   <a href="#" id="a_0d3952a1d4fa11e9b14000163c8b9390" onclick="onClickAction('2019-09','0d3952a1d4fa11e9b14000163c8b9390')">[收起]</a>
<div class="collector_content" id="div_0d3952a1d4fa11e9b14000163c8b9390" onclick="onClickAction('2019-09','0d3952a1d4fa11e9b14000163c8b9390')">
<p>“秃”如其来的年轻人“引爆”了在国内不温不火发展了近20年的植发生意。<span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">电梯、</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">户外大屏、</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">电视剧贴片、信息流、短视频社区......等媒介已悄然被植发广告占据，且热度不减。</span></p><p><strong><span style="font-family:PingFang SC, Lantinghei SC, Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Arial, Microsoft YaHei, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, WenQuanYi Zen Hei, WenQuanYi Micro Hei, sans-serif">各品牌方加足马力进行广告推广背后，是行业竞争的急速加剧</span></strong><span style="font-family:PingFang SC, Lantinghei SC, Helvetica Neue, SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">、</span><a href="https://36kr.com/p/5148188" target="_blank" style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, sans-serif;">科</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">9月9日，</span><span &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">正式对外公布旗下<strong>“科发源微针植发”</strong>品牌更名为<strong>“大麦微针植发”</strong>（以下均简称为：大麦），放眼全球市场。</span></p><p><img src="https://pic.36krcnd.com/201909/11223629/um22uujiapbfgqbb.jpg!heading" data-img-size-val="1443,1080"/></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;"></span></p><p class="img-desc">大麦微针植发直营机构</p><h3 label="二级标题" style="">更名背后的全球化战略</h3><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">发展了二十余年，在行业也建立了一定影响力，何以“壮士断腕”？</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">李兴东表示，“此次品牌更名是经过深思熟虑的重大决定，筹备了一年半，新品牌也是从数千个品牌名称中精心挑选出来的”；之所以最终选用“大麦”，除了简单、易记之外，还包含了“让发友们的头发能像大麦一样茂密繁盛”的寓意。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">此前，在「大麦」战略顾问特劳特的多次品牌调研中，都出现了<strong>用户很难记住及记准确的问题，直接导致广告效果收效甚微</strong>，多数客户都来自转介绍或口碑，“从一个月几台手术逐渐到一月几千例手术，这个过程我们用了5年”。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">而真正触动团队做出最终决定的还是海外拓展的“初次败北”。据他介绍，集团</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">在2018年10月在美国芝加哥开了第一家分院——中国首家海外植发机构，根据音译创造了“Kafuring”一词</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">，“很多外国朋友根本不认识，为避免在全球化发展中出现类似问题，品牌升级势在必行”。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">根据规划，</span><strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">未来3年，「大麦」</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">要在海外新增20+大麦微针植发机构——</span></strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">目前已启动在泰国、新加坡、马来西亚等国的筹备工作</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">，</span><strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">在</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">全球合作10余家一流科研类机构和组织等</span></strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;"></span></p><p><img src="https://pic.36krcnd.com/201909/11234923/380uabj6q1l6ua1q.jpg!heading" data-img-size-val="1440,1080"/></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">按他的话说，“目前中国植发市场的空间将近千亿，我想全球市场可能是万亿”。</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">那海外市场真的这么好做吗？要知道，国内植发市场整体渗透率还很低，尚有太多存量待挖掘。</span><br/></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">李兴东坦言，</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">“其实现在毛发相关的需求量并没有显著增长，甚至和5/10年前一样大，不然，一些头部生发养发品牌不可能做到那么大”；</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">之所以现在如此火爆，主要还归功于植发技术效果立竿见影，需求被进一步激发出来。</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">另外，目前一二线城市植发机构的体量基本能满足既定需求，拓展空间有限；对下沉市场的需求是否有必要布局直营机构也还有待商榷——目前的应对方案是建立医生集团。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">他认为，随着赛道上新玩家的不断涌现，国内市场的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">发展速度一定不如早几年，“死磕”国内并非明智之举；相反地，“既然中国能在技术领域做得这么好，完全可以走向海外”</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">比较利好的是，国外（尤其是欧美）的<strong>办医环境和医生习惯更有利于机构实现良性发展</strong>。李兴东介绍：首先，在海外多数国家</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">开诊所必须是医生，更能和集团达成共识；其次，</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">欧美人手脚大，在“植发”这类细致工作上可能不如亚洲人，双方能互补</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">不过他也强调，此举除了拓展市场，<strong>更多是能和很多科研机构达成合作，让「大麦」的植发技术走在世界前列</strong>。举例来说，其海外分院院长卡洛斯教授就曾受邀参与国际毛发行业尖端科研项目“冷冻毛囊克隆”的科研组。</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">特劳特（大麦战略顾问）全球总裁邓德隆则补充说道，这也是为了更改</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">企业的经营方式，即</span><strong style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">主动舍弃一些低端产品线和传统的植发方式，全面替换为效果和体验更好的微针植发</strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;"></span></p><h3 label="二级标题" style="">用前沿技术和专业医生团队建起“护城河”</h3><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">36氪了解到，「大麦」最早由北京长虹医院的承包科室起家，由外科专家邹建红和毛发移植专家李兴东共同创建，是<strong>国内民营植发医院中唯一一个医生出身的创始团队</strong>，也是对技术最孜孜以求的团队。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;"></span></p><p>1997年，李兴东便从美国引进自体毛囊移植技术（FUT)，在国内首批开展毛发移植技术治疗脱发，此后国内其他植发机构才纷纷入场；<span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">2004年，「大麦」研发的“自体毛囊移植器A”和 “自体毛囊移植器B”同时获得国家专利，这是国内毛发移植界首次拥有自主研发的专利技术；</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">2006年，「大麦」从美国引进微针植发技术，彼时国内普遍传采用统镊子植发技术；技术引进后，「大麦」花费了12年进行革新并结合中国人的头皮环境加以改良，现已经历4次换代，并获得了相应国家专利。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;"></span></p><p><img src="https://pic.36krcnd.com/201909/11231602/iped0s22usj44o3c.gif" data-img-size-val="520,400"/></p><p class="img-desc">微针植发技术（来自<a href="http://blog.sina.com.cn/s/blog_1995c5e240102yjfi.html" target="_blank">百度</a>）</p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">据李兴东介绍，相对于传统植发，微针技术的种植孔要小三分之一，对头皮创伤小、恢复快，同等面积下植发密度更高；还可360度灵活掌控头发的生长方向，能实现精准种植，术后效果更加自然。他透露，</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">目前其它机构</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">在微针植发技术上</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">普遍应用较少，而</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">「大麦」已经实现了普及，因为“应用技术瓶颈的突破和医生操作习惯的改变都需要时间来磨合，至少需要1年半”</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">李兴东透露，<strong>目前公司的研发投入能占到销售收入的5-10%</strong>，“在国内绝对属于前列”；最近还</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">和南方医科大学发起了</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">中国人群雄激素源性脱发易感基因的挖掘与数据库构建的相关项目，以及与机器人植发公司ARTAS达成了中国独家战略合作，</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">想在前沿技术探索和改善植发方式上“快人一步”。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">他认为，</span><strong><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">民营医疗机构发展离不开服务，在服务水平上大家普遍相差不大，但</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">技术能代表效果，要想长远发展，一定要牢牢抓住技术。</span></strong></p><p>当然，有好的技术没有严格的操作把控还不行，毕竟不正规机构/美容院开展植发手术、无证行医等乱象早已不是新鲜事。<span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">李兴东告诉36氪，「大麦」的医生都必须具备临床医学背景和</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">外科基础，后续会在总部进行统一培训，</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">之后会有严格考核，达标后才能走上工作岗位，后续会逐年进行考核并进行等级划分。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">为避免过度医疗，</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">对于日常的医疗监管，「大麦」开设了一个分诊平台，只要严格符合植发手术诊断标准的顾客才能走进手术室，剩下的会建议重新诊断或药物治疗。他表示，“<strong>每年因此而拒绝掉的人，大概是每年已消费客户数2倍的量。</strong>”</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">基于此，「大麦」目前也配备了皮肤科医生，还支持三甲医院专家出诊，以确保对患者进行精确诊断。</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">要强调的是，植发是团队“作战”，</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">一个医生往往要配备五六个护士。对植发机构而言，稳定的团队尤为重要，而目前，<strong>「大麦」做到了“技术人员基本没有流失”</strong></span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">。</span></p><h3 label="二级标题" style="">抢夺用户心智的时代已经到来</h3><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">伴随着技术更迭的还有行业的显著变化。</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">作为一线从业者，</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">李兴东的一个明显感受就是“</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">广告多了、机构多了、从业人员多了，高校和科研院越来多地承担相关的科教研任务</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">”</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">在全新的市场环境冲击下，「大麦」也面临着全新的挑战，尤其是在对家都相继拿到巨额投资后。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">李兴东表示，资本入局对植发行业的发展有助力作用，包括对规模发展、开店速度、团队搭建等；但问题是，引进资本后如何发展。他希望资本只是参股而非绝对控股，因为资本和医生有天然的“隔阂”，需要看到植发行业的医疗本质和发展瓶颈。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">不过，李兴东也无奈表示，现在头部企业都在大肆铺广告，<strong>「大麦」为跟上这个步伐，进行融资扩张也就成了一条必由之路</strong>，毕竟现在早已不是</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">酒香不怕巷子深的时代了。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">根据邓德隆的观点，中国的商业竞争通常要经过三个阶段：最早是供应端的战争，即谁能提供相对优质的供应谁就会取得胜利，植发初期往往供不应求，不需要广告和定位；随着行业玩家的增多，渠道端成了核心，掌握多少终端网点、有多少医务人员提供服务成为新的优势；接着，<strong>资本进入“催熟”市场，市场竞争进入第三阶段，也就是心智战争阶段</strong>。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">邓德隆认为，“只有建立心智优势，才能赢得品牌认知，有认知才有选择。”那</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">如何才能抢夺用户心智？「大麦」战略合作伙伴分众传媒CEO</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">江南春表示，从传播的角度，「大麦」要找到属于自己三位一体的定位，包括</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">对消费者特别有价值、消费者特别需求，以及和竞争对手形成核心差异，才能在广告上取得革命性成功，进行品牌提升和高密度的广告推广成了必然选择。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;"></span></p><p><img src="https://pic.36krcnd.com/201909/12003509/139tdufzw6j4jngl.jpg!heading" data-img-size-val="1080,1440"/></p><p label="图片描述" classname="img-desc" class="img-desc" style=""><span style="color: #999999; font-size: 12px; text-align: center; font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">大麦的分众电梯广告</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">与以往不同的是，<strong>「大麦」的广告主战场已从过去的百度变为分众传媒</strong>。李兴东透露，百度竞价广告已从过去的70%投入削减到现在不足30%，分众电梯广告现在成为了最主要的传播媒介。据</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">邓德隆介绍，</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">分众的优势在于：1）精准人群，即城市年轻人主流人群跟分众较贴合；2）转化率高，因为在</span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">信息接收碎片化时代，电梯作为必经空间能让用户主动收视。</span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;"></span></p><p><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Lantinghei SC&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, &quot;WenQuanYi Zen Hei&quot;, &quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;, sans-serif;">不过李兴东也强调，投放广告并非仅仅为了应对激烈的市场竞争，“毕竟植发市场（的竞争）远没有医美激烈”。他认为，之所以医美乱象频发，就是因为早先医美并不注重品牌建设；相反地，植发市场已有几家机构进入第一梯队，<strong>是时候通过品牌推广教育用户、进入用户心智，避免重演医美“乱象”</strong>。</span></p><address><p><span style="font-family:PingFang SC, Lantinghei SC, Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Arial, Microsoft YaHei, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, WenQuanYi Zen Hei, WenQuanYi Micro Hei, sans-serif">延伸阅读</span></p></address><p><a href="https://36kr.com/p/5164502" target="_blank">36氪新风向 | 每6个中国人中就有1人脱发，客单价超2.5万元的“头部生意”了解下</a></p><p><span style="font-family:PingFang SC, Lantinghei SC, Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Arial, Microsoft YaHei, 微软雅黑, STHeitiSC-Light, simsun, 宋体, WenQuanYi Zen Hei, WenQuanYi Micro Hei, sans-serif"><a href="https://36kr.com/p/5163805" target="_blank">年轻人老是哀嚎脱发头秃，所以我们干脆走访了一圈植发机构</a></span></p>
